## Questions And Answers

### What is an e-commerce creative agent?

An e-commerce creative agent like Bandy AI automates the entire creative production process for online sellers. Instead of manually creating product images, videos, and marketing content, you simply chat with the AI agent, describe what you need, and it generates professional-quality visuals instantly.

### What is Bandy AI?

Bandy AI is the world's first AI creative agent designed specifically for e-commerce businesses. It combines advanced AI technology with chat-based interaction to help online sellers create UGC ads, product videos, and listing images without hiring photographers, models, or video editors.

### What makes Bandy AI different from other AI tools for e-commerce?

As an AI agent for e-commerce creatives, Bandy AI works through simple chat conversations. It can handle everything—from generating fashion models and switching poses to creating complete video ads and image sets. It's built for e-commerce, understanding product photography requirements and marketplace standards. To put it simply, Bandy AI agent is the only e-commerce creative tool you need.

### What types of content can I create with Bandy AI agent?

You can create UGC-style video ads, product showcase videos, on-model photography, lifestyle images, social media content, marketplace listings, email campaign visuals, and more. All optimized for conversion across different e-commerce platforms.

### How fast can I get my content with Bandy AI agent?

Most images are generated in under 30 seconds. Videos typically take 2-5 minutes. Compare that to weeks of waiting for traditional photography or influencer content.

### Is the content created by Bandy AI agent unique?

Yes, every piece of content is uniquely generated based on your specific instructions and products. You own full commercial rights to all content created with your account.

### Can I use Bandy AI's e-commerce creative agent for free?

Yes, Bandy AI offers a free trial so you can experience our e-commerce creative agent before committing. You can start creating product images, fashion models, and video ads right away. However, to scale your e-commerce content creation as your business grows, you'll need to upgrade to one of our paid plans.

### Which e-commerce platforms does Bandy AI agent support?

Bandy AI agent works with all major platforms including Shopify, Amazon, eBay, Etsy, WooCommerce, and social commerce channels like Instagram Shopping and TikTok Shop. Export in optimized formats for each platform's requirements.

### Is my product and customer data secure?

Yes. Bandy AI's e-commerce creative agent uses industry-standard encryption and strict access controls. All assets remain private to your account.
